(***************************************************************************************

 Left adjoint to substitution for the codomain

 The fibers of the codomain fibration are given by slice categories and the functors
 between them are given by taking the pullback. Each of these functors has a left adjoint,
 which is given by composition. In this file, we establish this fact.

 There are multiple ways to construct this adjoint. We construct the unit and counit
 of this adjunction directly rather than using universal arrows. The reason for doing
 so, is because we want the right adjoint of this functor to compute nicely. For that
 reason, we construct it explicitly. The advantage of having nice computational behavior
 of this right adjoint, is that it helps with verifying the Beck-Chevalley conditions.

 We also verify that the codomain fibration has dependent sums. The main work here lies
 in calculating the Beck-Chevalley map.

 Contents
 1. The left adjoint
 2. The unit
 3. The counit
 4. The triangle equalities
 5. The adjunction
 6. The Beck-Chevalley condition
 7. Dependent sums for the codomain

 ***************************************************************************************)
Require Import UniMath.Foundations.All.

Section CodomainLeftAdj.
  Context {C : category}
          (HC : Pullbacks C)
          {x y : C}
          (f : x --> y).

  (** * 1. The left adjoint *)
  
C: category
HC: Pullbacks C
x, y: C
f: C ⟦ x, y ⟧
functor_data (C / x) (C / y)

  
C: category
HC: Pullbacks C
x, y: C
f: C ⟦ x, y ⟧
functor_data (C / x) (C / y)

    
C: category
HC: Pullbacks C
x, y: C
f: C ⟦ x, y ⟧
C / x → C / y
C: category
HC: Pullbacks C
x, y: C
f: C ⟦ x, y ⟧
∏ a b : C / x, C / x ⟦ a, b ⟧ → C / y ⟦ ?F a, ?F b ⟧

    
C: category
HC: Pullbacks C
x, y: C
f: C ⟦ x, y ⟧
C / x → C / y
 exact (cod_fib_comp f).
    
C: category
HC: Pullbacks C
x, y: C
f: C ⟦ x, y ⟧
∏ a b : C / x,
C / x ⟦ a, b ⟧
→ C / y ⟦ cod_fib_comp f a, cod_fib_comp f b ⟧
 
C: category
HC: Pullbacks C

f: C ⟦ x, y ⟧
g₁, g₂: C / x
h: C / x ⟦ g₁, g₂ ⟧
C ⟦ cod_dom (cod_fib_comp f g₁),
cod_dom (cod_fib_comp f g₂) ⟧
C: category
HC: Pullbacks C
x, y: C
f: C ⟦ x, y ⟧
g₁, g₂: C / x
h: C / x ⟦ g₁, g₂ ⟧
?g · cod_mor (cod_fib_comp f g₂) =
cod_mor (cod_fib_comp f g₁)

      
C: category
HC: Pullbacks C
x, y: C
f: C ⟦ x, y ⟧
g₁, g₂: C / x
h: C / x ⟦ g₁, g₂ ⟧
C ⟦ cod_dom (cod_fib_comp f g₁),
cod_dom (cod_fib_comp f g₂) ⟧
 exact (dom_mor h).
      
C: category
HC: Pullbacks C
x, y: C
f: C ⟦ x, y ⟧
g₁, g₂: C / x
h: C / x ⟦ g₁, g₂ ⟧
dom_mor h · cod_mor (cod_fib_comp f g₂) =
cod_mor (cod_fib_comp f g₁)
 abstract
          (cbn ;
           rewrite !assoc ;
           rewrite mor_eq ;
           apply idpath).
  Defined.

      apply idpath.

# comp_functor_data (h₁ · h₂) =

  (# comp_functor_data h₁ · # comp_functor_data h₂)

      
C: category
HC: Pullbacks C
x, y: C
f: C ⟦ x, y ⟧

h₁: C / x ⟦ g₁, g₂ ⟧
h₂: C / x ⟦ g₂, g₃ ⟧
dom_mor (h₁ · h₂) =
dom_mor
  (make_cod_fib_mor (dom_mor h₁)
     (comp_functor_data_subproof g₁ g₂ h₁)
   · make_cod_fib_mor (dom_mor h₂)
       (comp_functor_data_subproof g₂ g₃ h₂))

      
C: category
HC: Pullbacks C
x, y: C
f: C ⟦ x, y ⟧
g₁, g₂, g₃: C / x
h₁: C / x ⟦ g₁, g₂ ⟧
h₂: C / x ⟦ g₂, g₃ ⟧
dom_mor h₁ · dom_mor h₂ =
dom_mor
  (make_cod_fib_mor (dom_mor h₁)
     (comp_functor_data_subproof g₁ g₂ h₁))
· dom_mor
    (make_cod_fib_mor (dom_mor h₂)
       (comp_functor_data_subproof g₂ g₃ h₂))

      apply idpath.
  Qed.

  (** * 2. The unit *)

HC: Pullbacks C
x, y: C
f: C ⟦ x, y ⟧
nat_trans_data (functor_identity (C / x))
  (comp_functor ∙ cod_pb HC f)

  
C: category
HC: Pullbacks C
x, y: C
f: C ⟦ x, y ⟧
nat_trans_data (functor_identity (C / x))
  (comp_functor ∙ cod_pb HC f)

HC: Pullbacks C
x, y: C
f: C ⟦ x, y ⟧
g: C / x
C ⟦ cod_dom (functor_identity (C / x) g),
cod_dom ((comp_functor ∙ cod_pb HC f) g) ⟧

?g · cod_mor ((comp_functor ∙ cod_pb HC f) g) =

HC: Pullbacks C
x, y: C
f: C ⟦ x, y ⟧
g: C / x
identity (cod_dom g) · pr2 (comp_functor g) =
cod_mor g · f
 abstract
          (cbn ;
           apply id_left).
    
C: category
HC: Pullbacks C
x, y: C
f: C ⟦ x, y ⟧
g: C / x
PullbackArrow
  (HC y (pr1 (comp_functor g)) x
     (pr2 (comp_functor g)) f)
  (cod_dom (functor_identity (C / x) g))
  (identity (cod_dom g)) (cod_mor g)
  (comp_functor_unit_data_subproof g)
· cod_mor ((comp_functor ∙ cod_pb HC f) g) =
cod_mor (functor_identity (C / x) g)
 abstract
        (cbn ;
         rewrite PullbackArrow_PullbackPr2 ;
         apply idpath).
  Defined.

C: category
HC: Pullbacks C
x, y: C

# (functor_identity (C / x)) h
· comp_functor_unit_data g₂ =
comp_functor_unit_data g₁
· # (comp_functor ∙ cod_pb HC f) h

    
C: category
HC: Pullbacks C
x, y: C
f: C ⟦ x, y ⟧
g₁, g₂: C / x
h: C / x ⟦ g₁, g₂ ⟧
dom_mor
  (# (functor_identity (C / x)) h
   · comp_functor_unit_data g₂) =
dom_mor
  (comp_functor_unit_data g₁
   · # (comp_functor ∙ cod_pb HC f) h)

    
C: category
HC: Pullbacks C
x, y: C
f: C ⟦ x, y ⟧
g₁, g₂: C / x
h: C / x ⟦ g₁, g₂ ⟧
dom_mor (h · comp_functor_unit_data g₂) =
dom_mor
  (comp_functor_unit_data g₁
   · (cartesian_cod_disp_map
        (PullbackPr1
           (HC y (cod_dom g₂) x (cod_mor g₂ · f) f),,
         PullbackSqrCommutes
           (HC y (cod_dom g₂) x (cod_mor g₂ · f) f))
        (pr22 (HC y (cod_dom g₂) x (cod_mor g₂ · f) f))
        (identity x)
        (HC y (cod_dom g₁) x (cod_mor g₁ · f) f,,
         PullbackPr2
           (HC y (cod_dom g₁) x (cod_mor g₁ · f) f))
        (transportf
           (mor_disp
              (HC y (cod_dom g₁) x (cod_mor g₁ · f) f,,
               PullbackPr2
                 (HC y (cod_dom g₁) x (cod_mor g₁ · f)
                    f)) (cod_fib_comp f g₂))
           (id_right f @ ! id_left f)
           (PullbackPr1
              (HC y (cod_dom g₁) x (cod_mor g₁ · f) f)
            · dom_mor h,,
            cod_id_comp_subproof0 C x y y f
              (identity y)
              (HC y (cod_dom g₁) x (cod_mor g₁ · f) f,,
               PullbackPr2
                 (HC y (cod_dom g₁) x (cod_mor g₁ · f)
                    f)) (cod_fib_comp f g₁)
              (cod_fib_comp f g₂)
              (PullbackPr1
                 (HC y (cod_dom g₁) x (cod_mor g₁ · f)
                    f),,
               PullbackSqrCommutes
                 (HC y (cod_dom g₁) x (cod_mor g₁ · f)
                    f))
              (make_cod_fib_mor (dom_mor h)
                 (comp_functor_data_subproof g₁ g₂ h)))),,
      cartesian_cod_disp_comm_pr2
        (PullbackPr1
           (HC y (cod_dom g₂) x (cod_mor g₂ · f) f),,
         PullbackSqrCommutes
           (HC y (cod_dom g₂) x (cod_mor g₂ · f) f))
        (pr22 (HC y (cod_dom g₂) x (cod_mor g₂ · f) f))
        (identity x)
        (HC y (cod_dom g₁) x (cod_mor g₁ · f) f,,
         PullbackPr2
           (HC y (cod_dom g₁) x (cod_mor g₁ · f) f))
        (transportf
           (mor_disp
              (HC y (cod_dom g₁) x (cod_mor g₁ · f) f,,
               PullbackPr2
                 (HC y (cod_dom g₁) x (cod_mor g₁ · f)
                    f)) (cod_fib_comp f g₂))
           (id_right f @ ! id_left f)
           (PullbackPr1
              (HC y (cod_dom g₁) x (cod_mor g₁ · f) f)
            · dom_mor h,,
            cod_id_comp_subproof0 C x y y f
              (identity y)
              (HC y (cod_dom g₁) x (cod_mor g₁ · f) f,,
               PullbackPr2
                 (HC y (cod_dom g₁) x (cod_mor g₁ · f)
                    f)) (cod_fib_comp f g₁)
              (cod_fib_comp f g₂)
              (PullbackPr1
                 (HC y (cod_dom g₁) x (cod_mor g₁ · f)
                    f),,
               PullbackSqrCommutes
                 (HC y (cod_dom g₁) x (cod_mor g₁ · f)
                    f))
              (make_cod_fib_mor (dom_mor h)
                 (comp_functor_data_subproof g₁ g₂ h))))))

    
C: category
HC: Pullbacks C
x, y: C
f: C ⟦ x, y ⟧
g₁, g₂: C / x
h: C / x ⟦ g₁, g₂ ⟧
dom_mor h · dom_mor (comp_functor_unit_data g₂) =
dom_mor (comp_functor_unit_data g₁)
· dom_mor
    (cartesian_cod_disp_map
       (PullbackPr1
          (HC y (cod_dom g₂) x (cod_mor g₂ · f) f),,
        PullbackSqrCommutes
          (HC y (cod_dom g₂) x (cod_mor g₂ · f) f))
       (pr22 (HC y (cod_dom g₂) x (cod_mor g₂ · f) f))
       (identity x)
       (HC y (cod_dom g₁) x (cod_mor g₁ · f) f,,
        PullbackPr2
          (HC y (cod_dom g₁) x (cod_mor g₁ · f) f))
       (transportf
          (mor_disp
             (HC y (cod_dom g₁) x (cod_mor g₁ · f) f,,
              PullbackPr2
                (HC y (cod_dom g₁) x (cod_mor g₁ · f)
                   f)) (cod_fib_comp f g₂))
          (id_right f @ ! id_left f)
          (PullbackPr1
             (HC y (cod_dom g₁) x (cod_mor g₁ · f) f)
           · dom_mor h,,
           cod_id_comp_subproof0 C x y y f
             (identity y)
             (HC y (cod_dom g₁) x (cod_mor g₁ · f) f,,
              PullbackPr2
                (HC y (cod_dom g₁) x (cod_mor g₁ · f)
                   f)) (cod_fib_comp f g₁)
             (cod_fib_comp f g₂)
             (PullbackPr1
                (HC y (cod_dom g₁) x (cod_mor g₁ · f)
                   f),,
              PullbackSqrCommutes
                (HC y (cod_dom g₁) x (cod_mor g₁ · f)
                   f))
             (make_cod_fib_mor (dom_mor h)
                (comp_functor_data_subproof g₁ g₂ h)))),,
     cartesian_cod_disp_comm_pr2
       (PullbackPr1
          (HC y (cod_dom g₂) x (cod_mor g₂ · f) f),,
        PullbackSqrCommutes
          (HC y (cod_dom g₂) x (cod_mor g₂ · f) f))
       (pr22 (HC y (cod_dom g₂) x (cod_mor g₂ · f) f))
       (identity x)
       (HC y (cod_dom g₁) x (cod_mor g₁ · f) f,,
        PullbackPr2
          (HC y (cod_dom g₁) x (cod_mor g₁ · f) f))
       (transportf
          (mor_disp
             (HC y (cod_dom g₁) x (cod_mor g₁ · f) f,,
              PullbackPr2
                (HC y (cod_dom g₁) x (cod_mor g₁ · f)
                   f)) (cod_fib_comp f g₂))
          (id_right f @ ! id_left f)
          (PullbackPr1
             (HC y (cod_dom g₁) x (cod_mor g₁ · f) f)
           · dom_mor h,,
           cod_id_comp_subproof0 C x y y f
             (identity y)
             (HC y (cod_dom g₁) x (cod_mor g₁ · f) f,,
              PullbackPr2
                (HC y (cod_dom g₁) x (cod_mor g₁ · f)
                   f)) (cod_fib_comp f g₁)
             (cod_fib_comp f g₂)
             (PullbackPr1
                (HC y (cod_dom g₁) x (cod_mor g₁ · f)
                   f),,
              PullbackSqrCommutes
                (HC y (cod_dom g₁) x (cod_mor g₁ · f)
                   f))
             (make_cod_fib_mor (dom_mor h)
                (comp_functor_data_subproof g₁ g₂ h)))))

    
C: category
HC: Pullbacks C
x, y: C
f: C ⟦ x, y ⟧
g₁, g₂: C / x
h: C / x ⟦ g₁, g₂ ⟧
dom_mor h
· PullbackArrow
    (HC y (cod_dom g₂) x (cod_mor g₂ · f) f)
    (cod_dom g₂) (identity (cod_dom g₂)) (cod_mor g₂)
    (comp_functor_unit_data_subproof g₂) =
PullbackArrow (HC y (cod_dom g₁) x (cod_mor g₁ · f) f)
  (cod_dom g₁) (identity (cod_dom g₁)) (cod_mor g₁)
  (comp_functor_unit_data_subproof g₁)
· cartesian_cod_disp_map
    (PullbackPr1
       (HC y (cod_dom g₂) x (cod_mor g₂ · f) f),,
     PullbackSqrCommutes
       (HC y (cod_dom g₂) x (cod_mor g₂ · f) f))
    (pr22 (HC y (cod_dom g₂) x (cod_mor g₂ · f) f))
    (identity x)
    (HC y (cod_dom g₁) x (cod_mor g₁ · f) f,,
     PullbackPr2
       (HC y (cod_dom g₁) x (cod_mor g₁ · f) f))
    (transportf
       (mor_disp
          (HC y (cod_dom g₁) x (cod_mor g₁ · f) f,,
           PullbackPr2
             (HC y (cod_dom g₁) x (cod_mor g₁ · f) f))
          (cod_fib_comp f g₂))
       (id_right f @ ! id_left f)
       (PullbackPr1
          (HC y (cod_dom g₁) x (cod_mor g₁ · f) f)
        · dom_mor h,,
        cod_id_comp_subproof0 C x y y f (identity y)
          (HC y (cod_dom g₁) x (cod_mor g₁ · f) f,,
           PullbackPr2
             (HC y (cod_dom g₁) x (cod_mor g₁ · f) f))
          (cod_fib_comp f g₁) (cod_fib_comp f g₂)
          (PullbackPr1
             (HC y (cod_dom g₁) x (cod_mor g₁ · f) f),,
           PullbackSqrCommutes
             (HC y (cod_dom g₁) x (cod_mor g₁ · f) f))
          (make_cod_fib_mor (dom_mor h)
             (comp_functor_data_subproof g₁ g₂ h))))

    
C: category
HC: Pullbacks C
x, y: C
f: C ⟦ x, y ⟧
g₁, g₂: C / x
h: C / x ⟦ g₁, g₂ ⟧
dom_mor h
· PullbackArrow
    (HC y (cod_dom g₂) x (cod_mor g₂ · f) f)
    (cod_dom g₂) (identity (cod_dom g₂)) (cod_mor g₂)
    (comp_functor_unit_data_subproof g₂)
· PullbackPr1 (HC y (cod_dom g₂) x (cod_mor g₂ · f) f) =
PullbackArrow (HC y (cod_dom g₁) x (cod_mor g₁ · f) f)
  (cod_dom g₁) (identity (cod_dom g₁)) (cod_mor g₁)
  (comp_functor_unit_data_subproof g₁)
· cartesian_cod_disp_map
    (PullbackPr1
       (HC y (cod_dom g₂) x (cod_mor g₂ · f) f),,

           (PullbackPr1 (HC y (pr1 g₁) x (pr2 g₁) f)
            · pr1 h,,
            cod_id_comp_subproof0 C x y y f
              (identity y)
              (HC y (pr1 g₁) x (pr2 g₁) f,,
               PullbackPr2
                 (HC y (pr1 g₁) x (pr2 g₁) f)) g₁ g₂
              (PullbackPr1
                 (HC y (pr1 g₁) x (pr2 g₁) f),,
               PullbackSqrCommutes
                 (HC y (pr1 g₁) x (pr2 g₁) f)) h)))
     (comp_functor_data_subproof
        (HC y (pr1 g₁) x (pr2 g₁) f,,
         PullbackPr2 (HC y (pr1 g₁) x (pr2 g₁) f))
        (HC y (pr1 g₂) x (pr2 g₂) f,,
         PullbackPr2 (HC y (pr1 g₂) x (pr2 g₂) f))
        (cartesian_cod_disp_map
           (PullbackPr1 (HC y (pr1 g₂) x (pr2 g₂) f),,
            PullbackSqrCommutes
              (HC y (pr1 g₂) x (pr2 g₂) f))
           (pr22 (HC y (pr1 g₂) x (pr2 g₂) f))
           (identity x)
           (HC y (pr1 g₁) x (pr2 g₁) f,,
            PullbackPr2 (HC y (pr1 g₁) x (pr2 g₁) f))
           (transportf
              (mor_disp
                 (HC y (pr1 g₁) x (pr2 g₁) f,,
                  PullbackPr2
                    (HC y (pr1 g₁) x (pr2 g₁) f)) g₂)
              (id_right f @ ! id_left f)
              (PullbackPr1
                 (HC y (pr1 g₁) x (pr2 g₁) f) · pr1 h,,
               cod_id_comp_subproof0 C x y y f
                 (identity y)
                 (HC y (pr1 g₁) x (pr2 g₁) f,,
                  PullbackPr2
                    (HC y (pr1 g₁) x (pr2 g₁) f)) g₁
                 g₂
                 (PullbackPr1
                    (HC y (pr1 g₁) x (pr2 g₁) f),,
                  PullbackSqrCommutes
                    (HC y (pr1 g₁) x (pr2 g₁) f)) h)),,
         cartesian_cod_disp_comm_pr2
           (PullbackPr1 (HC y (pr1 g₂) x (pr2 g₂) f),,
            PullbackSqrCommutes
              (HC y (pr1 g₂) x (pr2 g₂) f))
           (pr22 (HC y (pr1 g₂) x (pr2 g₂) f))
           (identity x)
           (HC y (pr1 g₁) x (pr2 g₁) f,,
            PullbackPr2 (HC y (pr1 g₁) x (pr2 g₁) f))
           (transportf
              (mor_disp
                 (HC y (pr1 g₁) x (pr2 g₁) f,,
                  PullbackPr2
                    (HC y (pr1 g₁) x (pr2 g₁) f)) g₂)
              (id_right f @ ! id_left f)
              (PullbackPr1
                 (HC y (pr1 g₁) x (pr2 g₁) f) · pr1 h,,
               cod_id_comp_subproof0 C x y y f
                 (identity y)
                 (HC y (pr1 g₁) x (pr2 g₁) f,,
                  PullbackPr2

                 g₂
                 (PullbackPr1
                    (HC y (pr1 g₁) x (pr2 g₁) f),,
                  PullbackSqrCommutes
                    (HC y (pr1 g₁) x (pr2 g₁) f)) h))))
   · comp_functor_counit_data g₂) =
dom_mor (comp_functor_counit_data g₁ · h)

           comp_functor_unit,, comp_functor_counit))
       (adjcounit
          (comp_functor,,
           cod_pb HC f,,
           comp_functor_unit,, comp_functor_counit) g))
· PullbackPr1 (HC y (pr1 g) x (pr2 g) f) =

        (comp_functor,,
         cod_pb HC f,,
         comp_functor_unit,, comp_functor_counit) g))
· PullbackPr1 (HC y (pr1 g) x (pr2 g) f)

Arguments comp_functor_unit_data {C} HC {x y} f /.
Arguments comp_functor_counit_data {C} HC {x y} f /.

(** * 6. The Beck-Chevalley condition *)
Section BeckChevalley.
  Context {C : category}
          (HC : Pullbacks C)
          {w x y z : C}
          (f : x --> w)
          (g : y --> w)
          (h : z --> y)
          (k : z --> x)
          (p : k · f = h · g)
          (H : isPullback p).

  Let HD : cleaving (disp_codomain C) := disp_codomain_cleaving HC.
  Let P : Pullback f g := make_Pullback _ H.

  
C: category
HC: Pullbacks C
w, x, y, z: C
f: C ⟦ x, w ⟧
g: C ⟦ y, w ⟧
h: C ⟦ z, y ⟧
k: C ⟦ z, x ⟧
p: k · f = h · g
H: isPullback p
HD:= disp_codomain_cleaving HC: cleaving (disp_codomain C)
P:= make_Pullback p H: Pullback f g
φ: C / x
C ⟦ cod_dom (cod_pb HC k φ),

     (pr2 (cod_fib_comp f φ)) g)

  (PullbackPr2 (HC x (pr1 φ) z (pr2 φ) k) · h)

        (HC w (pr1 (cod_fib_comp f φ)) y

     (cod_left_beck_chevalley_mor_inv_subproof φ)
   · PullbackPr1 P) = ?b

g: C ⟦ y, w ⟧
h: C ⟦ z, y ⟧
k: C ⟦ z, x ⟧
p: k · f = h · g
H: isPullback p
HD:= disp_codomain_cleaving HC: cleaving (disp_codomain C)
P:= make_Pullback p H: Pullback f g
φ: C / x
is_inverse_in_precat (cod_left_beck_chevalley_mor φ)
  ?g

    
C: category
HC: Pullbacks C
w, x, y, z: C
f: C ⟦ x, w ⟧
g: C ⟦ y, w ⟧
h: C ⟦ z, y ⟧
k: C ⟦ z, x ⟧
p: k · f = h · g
H: isPullback p
HD:= disp_codomain_cleaving HC: cleaving (disp_codomain C)
P:= make_Pullback p H: Pullback f g
φ: C / x
C ⟦ cod_dom (cod_pb HC g (cod_fib_comp f φ)),
cod_dom (cod_pb HC k φ) ⟧
 exact (cod_left_beck_chevalley_mor_inv φ).

C: category
HC: Pullbacks C
w, x, y, z: C
f: C ⟦ x, w ⟧
g: C ⟦ y, w ⟧
h: C ⟦ z, y ⟧
k: C ⟦ z, x ⟧
p: k · f = h · g
H: isPullback p
HD:= disp_codomain_cleaving HC: cleaving (disp_codomain C)
P:= make_Pullback p H: Pullback f g
φ: C / x
cod_left_beck_chevalley_mor φ =
dom_mor
  (left_beck_chevalley_nat_trans
     (is_right_adjoint_cod_fiber_functor HC f)
     (is_right_adjoint_cod_fiber_functor HC h)
     (comm_nat_z_iso HD f g h k p) φ)

  (left_beck_chevalley_nat_trans

C: category
HC: Pullbacks C
w, x, y, z: C
f: C ⟦ x, w ⟧
g: C ⟦ y, w ⟧
h: C ⟦ z, y ⟧
k: C ⟦ z, x ⟧
p: k · f = h · g
H: isPullback p
HD:= disp_codomain_cleaving HC: cleaving (disp_codomain C)
P:= make_Pullback p H: Pullback f g
φ: C / x
dom_mor
  (# (left_adjoint
        (is_right_adjoint_cod_fiber_functor HC h))
     (# (fiber_functor_from_cleaving (disp_codomain C)
           HD k)
        (unit_from_right_adjoint
           (is_right_adjoint_cod_fiber_functor HC f) φ))
   · # (left_adjoint
          (is_right_adjoint_cod_fiber_functor HC h))
       (comm_nat_z_iso HD f g h k p
          (left_adjoint
             (is_right_adjoint_cod_fiber_functor HC f)
             φ))
   · counit_from_right_adjoint
       (is_right_adjoint_cod_fiber_functor HC h)
       (fiber_functor_from_cleaving (disp_codomain C)
          HD g
          (left_adjoint
             (is_right_adjoint_cod_fiber_functor HC f)
             φ))) = cod_left_beck_chevalley_mor φ

C: category
HC: Pullbacks C
w, x, y, z: C
f: C ⟦ x, w ⟧
g: C ⟦ y, w ⟧
h: C ⟦ z, y ⟧
k: C ⟦ z, x ⟧

P:= make_Pullback p H: Pullback f g
φ: C / x
PullbackArrow
  (HC x (HC w (cod_dom φ) x (cod_mor φ · f) f) z
     (PullbackPr2
        (HC w (cod_dom φ) x (cod_mor φ · f) f)) k)
  (HC x (pr1 φ) z (pr2 φ) k)
  (PullbackPr1 (HC x (pr1 φ) z (pr2 φ) k)
   · PullbackArrow
       (HC w (cod_dom φ) x (cod_mor φ · f) f)
       (cod_dom φ) (identity (cod_dom φ)) (cod_mor φ)
       (comp_functor_unit_data_subproof f φ))
  (PullbackPr2 (HC x (pr1 φ) z (pr2 φ) k))
  (cod_fiber_functor_pb_subproof HC z x k φ
     (HC w (cod_dom φ) x (cod_mor φ · f) f,,
      PullbackPr2
        (HC w (cod_dom φ) x (cod_mor φ · f) f))
     (make_cod_fib_mor
        (PullbackArrow
           (HC w (cod_dom φ) x (cod_mor φ · f) f)
           (cod_dom φ) (identity (cod_dom φ))
           (cod_mor φ)
           (comp_functor_unit_data_subproof f φ))
        (comp_functor_unit_data_subproof0 HC f φ))) =
?y'

      apply idpath.

           (cod_dom φ) (identity (cod_dom φ))
           (cod_mor φ)
           (comp_functor_unit_data_subproof f φ))
        (comp_functor_unit_data_subproof0 HC f φ)))
· dom_mor
    (# (left_adjoint
          (is_right_adjoint_cod_fiber_functor HC h))
       (comm_nat_z_iso HD f g h k p
          (left_adjoint
             (is_right_adjoint_cod_fiber_functor HC f)
             φ)))
· PullbackPr1
    (HC y (HC w (cod_dom φ) y (cod_mor φ · f) g) z
       (PullbackPr2
          (HC w (cod_dom φ) y (cod_mor φ · f) g)) h) =

k: C ⟦ z, x ⟧
p: k · f = h · g
H: isPullback p
HD:= disp_codomain_cleaving HC: cleaving (disp_codomain C)
P:= make_Pullback p H: Pullback f g
φ: C / x
PullbackArrow
  (HC x (HC w (cod_dom φ) x (cod_mor φ · f) f) z
     (PullbackPr2
        (HC w (cod_dom φ) x (cod_mor φ · f) f)) k)
  (HC x (pr1 φ) z (pr2 φ) k)
  (PullbackPr1 (HC x (pr1 φ) z (pr2 φ) k)
   · PullbackArrow
       (HC w (cod_dom φ) x (cod_mor φ · f) f)
       (cod_dom φ) (identity (cod_dom φ)) (cod_mor φ)
       (comp_functor_unit_data_subproof f φ))
  (PullbackPr2 (HC x (pr1 φ) z (pr2 φ) k))
  (cod_fiber_functor_pb_subproof HC z x k φ
     (HC w (cod_dom φ) x (cod_mor φ · f) f,,
      PullbackPr2
        (HC w (cod_dom φ) x (cod_mor φ · f) f))
     (make_cod_fib_mor
        (PullbackArrow
           (HC w (cod_dom φ) x (cod_mor φ · f) f)
           (cod_dom φ) (identity (cod_dom φ))
           (cod_mor φ)
           (comp_functor_unit_data_subproof f φ))
        (comp_functor_unit_data_subproof0 HC f φ)))
· (PullbackArrow
     (HC w (cod_dom φ) z (cod_mor φ · f) (k · f))
     (HC x (HC w (cod_dom φ) x (cod_mor φ · f) f) z
        (PullbackPr2
           (HC w (cod_dom φ) x (cod_mor φ · f) f)) k)
     (PullbackPr1
        (HC x (HC w (cod_dom φ) x (cod_mor φ · f) f) z
           (PullbackPr2
              (HC w (cod_dom φ) x (cod_mor φ · f) f))
           k)
      · PullbackPr1
          (HC w (cod_dom φ) x (cod_mor φ · f) f))
     (PullbackPr2
        (HC x (HC w (cod_dom φ) x (cod_mor φ · f) f) z
           (PullbackPr2
              (HC w (cod_dom φ) x (cod_mor φ · f) f))
           k))
     (cod_fiber_functor_from_cleaving_comp_mor_subproof
        HC z x w k f (cod_fib_comp f φ))
   · (PullbackArrow
        (HC w (cod_dom φ) z (cod_mor φ · f) (h · g))
        (HC w (cod_dom φ) z (cod_mor φ · f) (k · f))
        (PullbackPr1
           (HC w (cod_dom φ) z (cod_mor φ · f) (k · f)))
        (PullbackPr2
           (HC w (cod_dom φ) z (cod_mor φ · f) (k · f)))
        (cod_fiber_functor_on_eq_mor_subproof HC z w
           (k · f) (h · g) p (cod_fib_comp f φ))
      · PullbackArrow
          (HC w (cod_dom φ) y (cod_mor φ · f) g)
          (HC w (cod_dom φ) z (cod_mor φ · f) (h · g))
          (PullbackPr1
             (HC w (cod_dom φ) z (cod_mor φ · f)
                (h · g)))
          (PullbackPr2
             (HC w (cod_dom φ) z (cod_mor φ · f)
                (h · g)) · h)
          (cod_fiber_functor_from_cleaving_comp_mor_inv_subproof
             HC z y w h g (cod_fib_comp f φ))))
· PullbackPr1
    (HC w (pr1 (cod_fib_comp f φ)) y
       (pr2 (cod_fib_comp f φ)) g) =
PullbackArrow
  (HC w (pr1 (cod_fib_comp f φ)) y
     (pr2 (cod_fib_comp f φ)) g)
  (cod_dom (cod_pb HC k φ))
  (PullbackPr1 (HC x (pr1 φ) z (pr2 φ) k))
  (PullbackPr2 (HC x (pr1 φ) z (pr2 φ) k) · h)
  (cod_left_beck_chevalley_mor_subproof φ)
· PullbackPr1
    (HC w (pr1 (cod_fib_comp f φ)) y
       (pr2 (cod_fib_comp f φ)) g)

HD:= disp_codomain_cleaving HC: cleaving (disp_codomain C)
P:= make_Pullback p H: Pullback f g
φ: C / x
?b = PullbackPr1 (HC x (pr1 φ) z (pr2 φ) k)

      
C: category
HC: Pullbacks C
w, x, y, z: C
f: C ⟦ x, w ⟧
g: C ⟦ y, w ⟧
h: C ⟦ z, y ⟧
k: C ⟦ z, x ⟧
p: k · f = h · g
H: isPullback p
HD:= disp_codomain_cleaving HC: cleaving (disp_codomain C)
P:= make_Pullback p H: Pullback f g
φ: C / x
PullbackArrow
  (HC x (HC w (cod_dom φ) x (cod_mor φ · f) f) z
     (PullbackPr2
        (HC w (cod_dom φ) x (cod_mor φ · f) f)) k)
  (HC x (pr1 φ) z (pr2 φ) k)
  (PullbackPr1 (HC x (pr1 φ) z (pr2 φ) k)
   · PullbackArrow
       (HC w (cod_dom φ) x (cod_mor φ · f) f)
       (cod_dom φ) (identity (cod_dom φ)) (cod_mor φ)
       (comp_functor_unit_data_subproof f φ))
  (PullbackPr2 (HC x (pr1 φ) z (pr2 φ) k))
  (cod_fiber_functor_pb_subproof HC z x k φ
     (HC w (cod_dom φ) x (cod_mor φ · f) f,,
      PullbackPr2
        (HC w (cod_dom φ) x (cod_mor φ · f) f))
     (make_cod_fib_mor
        (PullbackArrow
           (HC w (cod_dom φ) x (cod_mor φ · f) f)
           (cod_dom φ) (identity (cod_dom φ))
           (cod_mor φ)
           (comp_functor_unit_data_subproof f φ))
        (comp_functor_unit_data_subproof0 HC f φ)))
· (PullbackArrow
     (HC w (cod_dom φ) z (cod_mor φ · f) (k · f))
     (HC x (HC w (cod_dom φ) x (cod_mor φ · f) f) z
        (PullbackPr2
           (HC w (cod_dom φ) x (cod_mor φ · f) f)) k)
     (PullbackPr1
        (HC x (HC w (cod_dom φ) x (cod_mor φ · f) f) z
           (PullbackPr2
              (HC w (cod_dom φ) x (cod_mor φ · f) f))
           k)
      · PullbackPr1
          (HC w (cod_dom φ) x (cod_mor φ · f) f))
     (PullbackPr2
        (HC x (HC w (cod_dom φ) x (cod_mor φ · f) f) z
           (PullbackPr2
              (HC w (cod_dom φ) x (cod_mor φ · f) f))
           k))
     (cod_fiber_functor_from_cleaving_comp_mor_subproof
        HC z x w k f (cod_fib_comp f φ))
   · (PullbackArrow
        (HC w (cod_dom φ) z (cod_mor φ · f) (h · g))
        (HC w (cod_dom φ) z (cod_mor φ · f) (k · f))
        (PullbackPr1
           (HC w (cod_dom φ) z (cod_mor φ · f) (k · f)))
        (PullbackPr2
           (HC w (cod_dom φ) z (cod_mor φ · f) (k · f)))
        (cod_fiber_functor_on_eq_mor_subproof HC z w
           (k · f) (h · g) p (cod_fib_comp f φ))
      · (PullbackArrow
           (HC w (cod_dom φ) y (cod_mor φ · f) g)
           (HC w (cod_dom φ) z (cod_mor φ · f) (h · g))
           (PullbackPr1
              (HC w (cod_dom φ) z (cod_mor φ · f)
                 (h · g)))
           (PullbackPr2
              (HC w (cod_dom φ) z (cod_mor φ · f)
                 (h · g)) · h)
           (cod_fiber_functor_from_cleaving_comp_mor_inv_subproof
              HC z y w h g (cod_fib_comp f φ))
         · PullbackPr1
             (HC w (pr1 (cod_fib_comp f φ)) y
                (pr2 (cod_fib_comp f φ)) g)))) = ?b

PullbackArrow (HC w (cod_dom φ) y (cod_mor φ · f) g)
  (HC w (cod_dom φ) z (cod_mor φ · f) (h · g))

     (HC w (cod_dom φ) z (cod_mor φ · f) (h · g)))
  (PullbackPr2
     (HC w (cod_dom φ) z (cod_mor φ · f) (h · g)) · h)
  (cod_fiber_functor_from_cleaving_comp_mor_inv_subproof
     HC z y w h g (cod_fib_comp f φ))
· PullbackPr1
    (HC w (pr1 (cod_fib_comp f φ)) y
       (pr2 (cod_fib_comp f φ)) g) = ?t2

        apply PullbackArrow_PullbackPr1.

        (comp_functor_unit_data_subproof0 HC f φ)))
· (PullbackArrow
     (HC w (cod_dom φ) z (cod_mor φ · f) (k · f))
     (HC x (HC w (cod_dom φ) x (cod_mor φ · f) f) z
        (PullbackPr2
           (HC w (cod_dom φ) x (cod_mor φ · f) f)) k)
     (PullbackPr1
        (HC x (HC w (cod_dom φ) x (cod_mor φ · f) f) z
           (PullbackPr2
              (HC w (cod_dom φ) x (cod_mor φ · f) f))
           k)
      · PullbackPr1
          (HC w (cod_dom φ) x (cod_mor φ · f) f))
     (PullbackPr2
        (HC x (HC w (cod_dom φ) x (cod_mor φ · f) f) z
           (PullbackPr2
              (HC w (cod_dom φ) x (cod_mor φ · f) f))
           k))
     (cod_fiber_functor_from_cleaving_comp_mor_subproof
        HC z x w k f (cod_fib_comp f φ))
   · (PullbackArrow
        (HC w (cod_dom φ) z (cod_mor φ · f) (h · g))
        (HC w (cod_dom φ) z (cod_mor φ · f) (k · f))
        (PullbackPr1
           (HC w (cod_dom φ) z (cod_mor φ · f) (k · f)))
        (PullbackPr2
           (HC w (cod_dom φ) z (cod_mor φ · f) (k · f)))
        (cod_fiber_functor_on_eq_mor_subproof HC z w
           (k · f) (h · g) p (cod_fib_comp f φ))
      · (PullbackArrow
           (HC w (cod_dom φ) y (cod_mor φ · f) g)
           (HC w (cod_dom φ) z (cod_mor φ · f) (h · g))
           (PullbackPr1
              (HC w (cod_dom φ) z (cod_mor φ · f)
                 (h · g)))
           (PullbackPr2
              (HC w (cod_dom φ) z (cod_mor φ · f)
                 (h · g)) · h)
           (cod_fiber_functor_from_cleaving_comp_mor_inv_subproof
              HC z y w h g (cod_fib_comp f φ))
         · PullbackPr2
             (HC w (pr1 (cod_fib_comp f φ)) y
                (pr2 (cod_fib_comp f φ)) g)))) =
PullbackPr2 (HC x (pr1 φ) z (pr2 φ) k) · h

p: k · f = h · g
H: isPullback p
HD:= disp_codomain_cleaving HC: cleaving (disp_codomain C)
P:= make_Pullback p H: Pullback f g
φ: C / x
PullbackPr2 (HC x (pr1 φ) z (pr2 φ) k) =
PullbackPr2 (HC x (pr1 φ) z (pr2 φ) k)

      apply idpath.
  Qed.

g: C ⟦ y, w ⟧
h: C ⟦ z, y ⟧
k: C ⟦ z, x ⟧
p: k · f = h · g
H: isPullback p
HD:= disp_codomain_cleaving HC: cleaving (disp_codomain C)
P:= make_Pullback p H: Pullback f g
left_beck_chevalley HD f g h k p
  (is_right_adjoint_cod_fiber_functor HC f)
  (is_right_adjoint_cod_fiber_functor HC h)

(** * 7. Dependent sums for the codomain *)

C: category
HC: Pullbacks C
HD:= disp_codomain_cleaving HC: cleaving (disp_codomain C)
has_dependent_sums HD


C: category
HC: Pullbacks C
HD:= disp_codomain_cleaving HC: cleaving (disp_codomain C)
has_dependent_sums HD

  
C: category
HC: Pullbacks C
HD:= disp_codomain_cleaving HC: cleaving (disp_codomain C)
∏ (x y : C) (f : C ⟦ x, y ⟧), dependent_sum HD f
C: category
HC: Pullbacks C
HD:= disp_codomain_cleaving HC: cleaving (disp_codomain C)
(λ L : ∏ (x y : C) (f : C ⟦ x, y ⟧),
       dependent_sum HD f,
 ∏ (w x y z : C) (f : C ⟦ x, w ⟧) (g : C ⟦ y, w ⟧)
 (h : C ⟦ z, y ⟧) (k : C ⟦ z, x ⟧)
 (p : k · f = h · g),
 isPullback p
 → left_beck_chevalley HD f g h k p (L x w f)
     (L z y h)) ?pr1

  
C: category
HC: Pullbacks C
HD:= disp_codomain_cleaving HC: cleaving (disp_codomain C)
∏ (x y : C) (f : C ⟦ x, y ⟧), dependent_sum HD f
 exact (λ x y f, is_right_adjoint_cod_fiber_functor HC f).
  
C: category
HC: Pullbacks C
HD:= disp_codomain_cleaving HC: cleaving (disp_codomain C)
(λ L : ∏ (x y : C) (f : C ⟦ x, y ⟧),
       dependent_sum HD f,
 ∏ (w x y z : C) (f : C ⟦ x, w ⟧) (g : C ⟦ y, w ⟧)
 (h : C ⟦ z, y ⟧) (k : C ⟦ z, x ⟧)
 (p : k · f = h · g),
 isPullback p
 → left_beck_chevalley HD f g h k p (L x w f)
     (L z y h))
  (λ (x y : C) (f : C ⟦ x, y ⟧),
   is_right_adjoint_cod_fiber_functor HC f)
 exact (λ w x y z f g h k p H, cod_left_beck_chevalley HC f g h k p H).
Defined.
